msg:My wife is a live shopping ******. She was amazed by the live broadcast of Yuewan by Azu of the WY team Bee Club. From then on, Yuewan became a place we must visit in our lifetime. After checking in at Yuewan, I really realized that "all the splendors are preludes", the weather is like this, the room is like this, and the mood is like this.
Before checking in, the enthusiastic Xiao Wu told us in advance that the projection screen had a minor malfunction due to the non-arrival of the repair parts when introducing the room we booked. After my wife showed a little dissatisfaction, Xiao Wu immediately contacted the front desk to change the room and took the trouble to show the changed room. Finally, our housekeeper Xiaopeng helped us upgrade the sea view pool room for free. From viewing the room, changing the room to upgrading, everything was so smooth and warm. After checking in, the clouds in the sky began to slowly increase and thicken. The sunset that night hid behind the layers of clouds and no longer showed up. I looked at my phone and learned that it would rain tomorrow. I felt very disappointed at the time. Will the most beautiful sunset in Yuewan pass us by? Fortunately, God still favored us. The sun shone on Erhai Lake in the morning of the second day, but it was not warm. The light was slanting, just right for taking pictures. In the afternoon, the rain curtain opened. Xiaopeng booked afternoon tea for us early. Sitting in the hotel cafe of Dali Internet celebrity, the sea and the distant mountains were shrouded in clouds and mist, and Cangshan Mountain appeared and disappeared from time to time, like a dream. In the evening, we came to Gansi Mido Yunnan Specialty Restaurant, which is also a Dali Internet celebrity, to have dinner. When we sat in the No. 8 dining table reserved by Xiaopeng for us, the sun miraculously shone obliquely through the dark clouds on the tableware and our faces, golden and bright, and we smiled at each other with relief. As soon as we finished the exquisitely presented and uniquely tasted Yunnan specialty meal, the proprietress urged us to go to the terrace and the pool to take pictures of the sunset. The Erhai Lake and Cangshan Mountain in front of us are so gentle and lovely. At this time, Erhai Lake has become a huge stage in seconds. Cangshan Mountain is like a giant screen background, and the sunset is the beautiful light of this giant stage. The people taking pictures are of course the protagonists in the center of the dream stage. Xiaopeng appeared behind us at some point, attentively and on time, and asked, "Can I take a photo for you?" Every beautiful photo and video still makes me excited and yearn for it, and I can't help but linger when I look at it! 
Thank you Yuewan! Thank you Xiaopeng, Xiaowu and all Yuewan employees! You gave us the best moments of our lives!
